The subject returns to Latveria and within weeks the public position is that the rescue was a tactical success of his sorcery, with no reference to his mother's words. Within months a new Midsummer ritual has been instituted — a *modified* version, now ostensibly to free other souls his mother had loved. The compulsive structure cannot tolerate the absence of its object and constructs a substitute.

The Strange relationship survives the episode and survives, more remarkably, the subject's later periods as Sorcerer Supreme during Strange's absences and exiles. Each transfer of the title is conducted with formal protocols; each return of the title is honored. Across the file this is the cleanest evidence of the *brittle but real code* — the patient's word, given to a recognized peer, is kept even when keeping it costs him.

## VIII. The Magical Maturations — Morgan, the Hood era, the cosmic-magic synthesis

The middle period is also where the subject's magical practice deepens past the level of inherited grimoire into something genuinely original: a hybrid sorcery-engineering discipline in which spells are designed, debugged, and version-controlled like software, and in which a sufficient enough machine can execute a ritual no human mage could sustain. This is the cognitive integration noted in the assessment — *magic and science are the same discipline at different scales* — and it is in the middle period that it bears its largest fruit.

The **Morgan le Fay alliance-and-rupture** is the romantic-magical centerpiece. He approaches her as a peer (the only woman in the file he approaches as such), conducts a brief and ambiguous courtship-collaboration, extracts what he requires, and exits. She regards him with a permanent hatred that he registers as flattering. There is no evidence the relationship was consummated in any conventional sense; there is significant evidence both believed it might have been, in some adjacent timeline.

The **Hood-era cabal** engagement, late-middle period, is instructive in the negative: he is offered a junior position in a villain-collective and declines with such immediate finality that the offer is treated by all subsequent collectives as a category error. He is constitutionally incapable of being a member of anything he does not lead.

## IX. The Wars

Across the middle period the subject is a combatant — at minimum a logistical principal — in roughly two dozen conflicts that meet the threshold of "war" rather than "engagement." The catalogue is too long for this section to fully render, but the pattern types recur:

- **Border wars with Symkaria.** Decades-long low-intensity, occasionally hot. The Silver Sable relationship within these conflicts is correct and professional — she is a competent woman conducting state business, which he respects, and the wars are conducted with relative restraint by his standards. He has never attempted to occupy Symkaria, despite the capability, because *occupation would require explanation*.

- **The Atlantean entanglements.** Variable. The Sub-Mariner is one of the few beings he genuinely respects without rivalry, perhaps because Namor's pride is structurally identical to his own and therefore not threatening — there is no asymmetry to resolve.

- **The Wakandan cold war.** Unresolved across the entire middle period. T'Challa is the rare peer-equal who *does not provoke* the rivalry response, possibly because T'Challa's competence is racially and culturally legible to the subject in a way Richards's is not (the Zefiro-Romani identification with a sovereign African state is real, and shows in trade policy and intelligence-sharing protocols that are unusually generous from the Latverian side). The brief and savage exchange in which the subject attempts to seize Wakandan vibranium reserves ends with mutual humiliation and a long quiet that both monarchs treat as the actual outcome.

- **The cosmic-tier engagements.** Multiple. Annihilation Wave logistics; the Skrull Secret Invasion period (during which the subject's intelligence services penetrate the Skrull network with notable efficiency, and during which he is *briefly imprisoned by Norman Osborn in the Raft* — an episode he refuses to discuss afterward and which generates a documented uptick in security perimeter expansion around Castle Doom for the subsequent eighteen months); the Reckoning War involvements; the various Galactus-adjacent crises.

The wars consolidate two operational findings. First, the subject's military doctrine is *attritional-elegant* — he prefers small forces, decisive technological asymmetry, and short campaigns; he despises sieges and avoids them where possible; he has never knowingly authorized civilian mass casualty even when it would be tactically advantageous. Second, the subject's diplomatic instincts are *better than his rivalry instincts* — when he negotiates as a head of state, he is patient, accurate, and remarkably willing to make concessions; when he negotiates as Doom-against-Richards, he is incapable of any of these qualities. **The patient becomes more functional the further he gets from the original wound.**

## X. The Mid-Period Drift in the Patterns

By the back half of the middle period the longitudinal patterns have evolved in specific, observable ways. A surveillance file would mark them as a drift curve.

- **Third-person speech increases in frequency**, not decreases. Early sovereign-period transcripts contain occasional first-person lapses; mid-period transcripts approach zero. The grammatical sequestration of "Victor" is becoming more total.

- **The mask is removed less often.** Boris's reports (when later partially recovered) suggest the unmasked face is seen by *no one* for stretches measured in years. The somatic identity is becoming more locked.

- **The Midsummer ritual extends in duration** from a single night to, eventually, the full week of Midsummer.

- **The Doombot population grows superlinearly.** By the end of the middle period the subject is increasingly mediated to the world by proxies, and the proxies are increasingly indistinguishable, by design, even to him.

- **The capacity for genuine attunement, paradoxically, does not atrophy** — it concentrates. The narrow circle (Boris, Kristoff in periods of détente, eventually Valeria Richards once she exists, the abstract Latverian peasant population) receives, if anything, *more* of the patient's actual care across the middle period than at its beginning. The available supply of tenderness is unchanged; the aperture has narrowed.

- **The self-sabotage signature stabilizes into a recognizable five-stage ladder** (catalogued in the Personality synthesis) and is, by the late middle period, *visible to his


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

*File segment covering approximately the last operational decade of the subject, with emphasis on the most recent twelve to thirty-six months. All entries cross-referenced to prior strata in the workup. This segment is the densest, because surveillance fidelity is highest here and because the patient's oscillations have accelerated.*

---

## 4.1 — Entry Point: The Post-Battleworld Reconstitution

The relevant recent window opens at the close of the *Secret Wars* (2015) arc, with the dissolution of Battleworld. The patient enters this period having occupied, for an unmeasured subjective duration, the position of literal god-emperor of a stitched multiverse, with the long-coveted domestic configuration installed (Sue Storm as consort, Franklin and Valeria as children, Reed Richards absent-presumed-dead). The patient *built* and *governed* this configuration competently for years of subjective time. The defining datum is the ending: when Reed proves to have survived and offers, in effect, a fair audit of the multiverse, the patient — having spent the entire arc denying that Reed could ever have done better — *concedes the point aloud*. The concession is brief, complete, and unwitnessed by any third party who could repeat it back to him.

This is the highest-integration moment in the longitudinal record. Surveillance assessment: the patient could not metabolize it. Within weeks of subjective re-entry into the restored 616 timeline, two compensations begin: (a) the unscarred face granted by Franklin Richards in the act of restoration is *kept* — a small concession to vanity, but more importantly an experimental probe — and (b) the patient retreats from the Latverian throne, which constitutes a controlled abdication of the most visible expression of his grandiose structure. Both moves are diagnostic. He is testing whether the structure survives without its two most public props (the face, the throne).

## 4.2 — The Unmasked Interregnum

Through this interval the patient operates publicly without the mask and without the country. He adopts armor of a different chassis, in different metals and colors, and conducts a vigilante practice oriented toward intercepting larger threats before they reach civilian scale. The behavioral content is genuinely altruistic in act; the *framing* is unstable. The patient narrates his actions in private monologue as proof of moral superiority to those he previously deemed peers — i.e., the altruism is recruited back into the grandiose project even as it is performed. Per the Pincus (2009) framework, this is textbook: the vulnerable-shame interior, briefly exposed by the *Secret Wars* concession, is being re-armored not by re-donning the literal mask but by erecting a *new* grandiose structure (hero-redeemer) in which he is again incomparable.

Two relational developments in this window deserve flagging.

**The Maker problem.** The patient enters into an oblique association with the evil-counterpart Reed Richards of the late Ultimate continuum — a being whose very existence is a metaphysical insult, in that it instantiates the proposition *Reed Richards can be worse than Doom*. The patient's tolerance of this entity, and willingness to be used by it in the cosmetic restoration of his face, indicates how desperately the experiment with the unscarred presentation was undertaken. He accepted aid from the one being in creation whose aid most explicitly proves that Richards-genius outclasses Doom-genius. He could not have done this if the grandiose defense were stable. It was not.

**Ben Grimm as audit.** The patient's interactions with Grimm during this window are unusually candid — Grimm being the only person who knew Victor before the construction of Doom, and who has no investment in either flattering or destroying him. The patient permits Grimm criticisms he permits no one else, then later denies the conversations. The *fact* of the denial confirms the conversations mattered.

## 4.3 — The Cosmetic Reversion

Within roughly twelve to eighteen months of operational time, the patient's unscarred face is lost again. The narrative pretext varies; the behavioral signature does not. *The patient cannot sustain a face that does not match the wound.* He arranges, accepts, or fails to prevent — the distinction is academic — a return to the disfigured presentation, and within hours of that return is back in the original mask, in the original chassis, speaking in the original third-person register. The interregnum is over. The surveillance verdict is unambiguous: the somatic identity is welded to the disfigurement at a level no cosmetic intervention can dislodge, because the disfigurement is not an injury he sustained — it is an injury he *administered to himself in order to be himself*. To remove it is to remove him. (Cross-ref: Medical §2, self-mutilation-in-service-of-identity-consolidation.)

## 4.4 — The Hellfire Gala Incident and the Brief Sovereignty of Krakoa

In the mutant-political theater of this period, the patient appears at the Hellfire Gala and at several adjacent diplomatic functions. His engagement with mutantdom is instrumental — he respects Xavier and Magneto as state-builders of comparable ambition and treats the Quiet Council as a peer-body, the only such body he has ever recognized that he did not create himself. His private assessment, reconstructable from the pattern of his interactions, is that the Krakoan project is structurally analogous to Latveria — sovereignty, technological uplift, citizen-loyalty — but undertaken by a class of beings whose biology has handed them advantages he had to forge. The envy is palpable and is converted, in his usual fashion, into condescension.

## 4.5 — The New York Mayoralty / Devil's Reign Period

The patient's response to a prolonged absence from the Latverian throne is to seek a *substitute throne in less defensible territory.* He maneuvers into the mayoralty of New York City during the period when Wilson Fisk's regime collapses. The episode is operationally clarifying for the file:

- The patient does not need New York. The patient needs *a throne*. Any throne. The withdrawal from Latveria has left a structural vacuum the grandiose defense cannot tolerate.
- He governs New York, briefly, in the same register he governs Latveria — orderly, repressive, technologically uplifted, paternalistic. The citizens' response is a mix of grudging compliance and genuine relief at the restoration of basic services, mirroring the Latverian pattern.
- He uses the position to wage a proxy campaign against the Fantastic Four. The proxy is transparent — the *fact* of being mayor permits him to issue lawful directives that constrain Richards. He is using municipal-administrative law as a continuation of the dominance contest by other means. The Reed fixation cannot be channeled out of him; it can only be re-channeled.
- The episode ends, predictably, with the patient back in Latveria. The detour cost him political capital and accomplished nothing strategic. The unconscious project — to occupy *a* sovereign position so that the public structure of his identity is not in deficit — succeeded for its duration.

Surveillance assessment: the willingness to take the New York position is one of the more revealing data points of the recent period. A stable grandiose structure does not need to slum it in municipal politics of a country it considers inferior. The patient took the job because he was, by his own standards, *unhoused* in identity terms. Cross-ref: Psychiatric §4, C-PTSD identity-alteration; the "Doom" self-state requires a throne to host it, and absent a throne the system destabilizes.

## 4.6 — The Reckoning War and the Re-Cosmic Phase

During the Reckoning War sequences the patient participates in a coalition response to a cosmic-scale threat and accedes — temporarily — to a higher-order arrangement in which he is not the apex. The cooperation is genuine and the contribution decisive. The patient demonstrates, again, that cosmic-scale altruism is within his behavioral repertoire when (a) the threat is large enough that participating does not connote subordination to a peer, and (b) the glory available for participation is substantial. (Cross-ref: Personality §5, "cosmic-scale altruism when it is *also* glorious.")

The post-engagement debrief — reconstructable from his communications in the period — shows the patient re-narrativizing the coalition victory as a Doom-led operation in which others were permitted to assist. The re-narrativization is unconvincing to anyone who was present and is not contested, because the participants have learned that contesting the narrative produces no benefit. He requires the narrative; they let him have it; the requirement is itself the diagnosis.

## 4.7 — The Reed-as-Doom Inversion

The most operationally significant recent development is the inversion event in which Reed Richards is, by metaphysical contrivance, installed in the Doom-position and Doom in the Richards-position. The patient's behavior across this inversion is profoundly informative:

- He does *not* enjoy the Richards-position. Surveillance had predicted he would; he is, after all, the man who has wanted Richards's life (family, scientific community, public regard) for sixty years.
- The actual occupancy of that life produces in him a measurable distress. He is most himself when he is opposed to Richards; the *opposition* is load-bearing in the structure. Take Reed away as antagonist and the patient does not know what to want.
- The arrangement reveals to him, in a way the *Secret Wars* concession did not, that the Reed fixation was never about replacing Reed. It was about being witnessed-as-superior *by* Reed. Replacement is not victory. Subordination of the witness is victory. You cannot subordinate a witness whose role you have taken.

The patient does not articulate this insight cleanly. It manifests behaviorally as a sustained agitation across the inversion period and a relieved settling back into the antagonistic configuration once the inversion is undone. The lesson is filed, denied, and partially retained.

## 4.8 — Ascension to Sorcerer Supreme

In the most recent period the patient inherits, by virtue of Strange's death and the magical-political mechanics of succession, the title of Sorcerer Supreme of the Earth dimension. This is, in narrative terms, an extraordinary elevation. In intelligence terms it is a stress test.

- The patient genuinely wanted this. The magical-science integration was always central to his cognitive style (Psychological §3, "Magic and science are the same discipline at different scales"); becoming the planet's chief sorcerer ratifies that integration cosmologically.
- The patient is *not* well-suited to the role's pastoral dimensions. The Sorcerer Supreme is, traditionally, a servant-position — a defender of a realm against threats the realm does not know it faces, with no acknowledgment expected. The patient cannot do unacknowledged service for long. He needs to be seen serving, or seen *not* serving and feared for the withholding.
- The patient also inherits, with the title, a relationship-debt to Strange (whose contest he won in *Triumph and Torment*, whose mother-rescue he was permitted in the same arc, whose mantle he now wears). The patient processes debt as humiliation; he will be looking for ways to discharge or repudiate it.
- The use of magic as primary modality reactivates the long-running ritual trauma load (Medical §2, annual Midsummer's ritual; mystical PTSD). His baseline arousal in the magical register is already elevated by attritional damage from decades of soul-bargaining. Adding the Supreme office to that substrate is, clinically, contraindicated. Behaviorally it produces a patient whose magical recklessness is dialed up and whose sleep, already minimal, contracts further.

Concurrent with the title, his cosmetic presentation shifts: the mask is amended with sorcerous overlays; the cloak elements borrowed from the Strange iconography are integrated into the Doom silhouette without surrendering the iconic profile. He has, characteristically, refused to wear the predecessor's regalia in unmodified form. He cannot wear a uniform he did not design.

## 4.9 — Domestic Configuration, Latveria, Current Quarter

Latveria under the patient's resumed direct rule is currently in a stable phase. The country's macro-indicators (low crime, infrastructure, public health, education) remain anomalously good for the region and for a polity its size. The repressive apparatus is intact and operating at maintenance levels rather than purge levels — a behavioral indicator that the patient does not currently feel internally threatened. (Latverian repression escalates when the patient's grandiose defense is destabilized; the country is a barometer.)

The Doombot fleet has been refreshed and partially redesigned to incorporate the new magical-supreme architecture. Several units appear to be running variant cognitive loads suggesting the patient is using them to externalize specific affective sub-routines he does not wish to host directly — a technological literalization of the dissociative identity-alteration logged in §3. The "Victor"/"Doom" split is being supplemented by a "Doom-prime"/"Doom-instances" split, with the instances permitted to fail in ways the prime is not. This is, in defensive terms, an *innovation*. It is also, in clinical terms, a worsening — externalized dissociation extends the architecture rather than reducing it.

Boris remains in service; his health and continuing presence appear to be a quiet anxiety the patient does not name. Kristoff's status is current-period unclear; the patient does not discuss him; surveillance interprets the silence as protective rather than estranged. Valeria Richards continues to be, idiosyncratically, the one external person granted unguarded warmth; correspondence between them (clandestine on her side, plausibly-deniable on his) continues at low frequency.

## 4.10 — Somatic and Behavioral Microsignals, Current

For the operational present, the following behavioral micro-pattern is logged as baseline:

- *Sleep:* two to three hours per twenty-four, distributed; magical sustenance supplementing biological. Trending downward.
- *Diet:* austere; single daily meal taken at variable hour; no shared meals except ceremonial. Wine ceremonially served, ceremonially not drunk by him.
- *Mask discipline:* unbroken in any company except, occasionally, with the bare-faced Latverian inner staff during private audiences, and even then only the lower mask is lifted, never fully removed; he has not allowed the upper-face mask to leave his skin in the presence of a witness for a documented interval of years.
- *Third-person register:* dominant in formal speech; first-person creeps in during late-night solitary work and in correspondence with Valeria Richards. The register shift is, by itself, a high-fidelity affect read.
- *Gait, in armor:* unchanged in twenty years; deliberate, slightly weighted forward, hands frequently clasped at the small of the back when stationary — a posture inherited from observed monarchs and consciously curated.
- *Vocal pattern:* baritone, slow, end-stopped phrases; questions answered after a calibrated pause designed to communicate that the question was beneath urgency.
- *Ritual annual:* the Midsummer's ritual to free his mother — *no longer performed*, since *Triumph and Torment*, the mother having been freed and having repudiated him. Per surveillance, the absent ritual has been replaced by an unstructured anniversary withdrawal on the same date each year, during which the patient is unavailable for several hours and after which Doombot activity briefly spikes in the surrounding region. This is grief, unmetabolized, displaced into hardware.
- *Reading:* heavy; technical, philosophical, occult; reads opponents' published works (Richards's papers, in particular) within hours of release, annotated returns sometimes mailed back.
- *Correspondence with Richards:* nonzero. Frequency variable. Content: ostensibly technical disputes; affectively, ongoing.

## 4.11 — Current Status, Summary Read

The patient is, at the moment of this dossier's compilation, in a *high-function, high-cost* configuration. The grandiose structure is intact and is being elaborated upward (new title, new powers, new architecture). The shame core is intact and is being neither addressed nor reduced. The new responsibilities (Sorcerer Supreme) impose servant-role demands he is constitutionally ill-equipped to meet, and the magical exposure they entail is loading further attritional damage onto a system that was already accumulating it.

The integration windows of the last decade — the *Secret Wars* concession, the unmasked interregnum, the Reed-inversion insight — have *all* been recorded, denied, and partially retained. "Partially retained" matters. The patient is not where he was twenty years ago. He has more integrated material available to him than at any previous period in the file; he has elaborated more sophisticated defenses against integrating it. The contest between these two trajectories is the live phenomenon of the current period.

Operationally: the patient is at his most productive when given a sufficiently large external threat, his most dangerous when shame-cued by a Richards-proximate stimulus, his most legible to surveillance when the third-person register slips, and his most accessible to intervention — should any such ever be contemplated — when in the presence of Valeria Richards, where the architecture briefly admits a witness whose recognition does not threaten him because she has known him, since infancy, as someone she is not required to fear.

He is, presently, on his throne, in his mask, in his country, with a new title, sleeping less, governing well, corresponding with his rival, performing a grief he no longer names, and waiting — though he would die before admitting it — to be properly seen.

— End Chronology IV. Proceed to next section.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: VICTOR VON DOOM

*Compiled from open-source canonical record (Lee/Kirby 1962–1970; Thomas, Englehart, Byrne, Stern/Mignola 1989; Waid 2003; Hickman 2009–2015; Bendis 2016–2018; Cates 2019; Zdarsky 2022; ancillary Latverian state medical archives reconstructed by inference). Cross-referenced with clinical sources cited in workup. This section maps the body — what has been done to it, what it has been made to do, and what each event installed in the mind that wears it.*

---

## 1. PRENATAL, NEONATAL, AND EARLY CHILDHOOD (Year 0 — ~Year 7)

**Genetic and gestational baseline.** Subject is the biological son of Werner von Doom (Zefiro healer; somatic profile: lean, ectomorphic, exceptional fine-motor) and Cynthia von Doom (Zefiro hedge-witch; somatic profile per surviving portraiture: small-framed, dark-eyed, hyperreactive sympathetic presentation consistent with chronic threat-living). No record of obstetric complication. The Zefiro encampment lacked institutional medical care; delivery was almost certainly by midwife in a wagon or tent under winter conditions.

**Early nutritional status.** Endemic Zefiro deprivation — caloric restriction, episodic protein insufficiency, no dental care, parasitic load typical of Carpathian itinerant populations of the period. Subject's adult height (canonically 6'2") and skeletal robustness indicate that whatever deprivation existed was not catastrophic, but late-childhood growth-plate radiographs (if extant) would likely show transverse Harris lines marking discrete episodes of hunger or febrile illness.

**Maternal loss (~age 6–7).** Cynthia's death by Latverian soldiery is the first documented somatic-witness trauma. The child was present or proximate. The body was not given to him for grieving; the soul, by his subsequent obsessional account, was *visibly* drawn down — i.e., the subject reports a perceptual experience that fused bereavement with damnation in a single ungrievable image. Whether the perception was veridical (his cosmos permits it) or hallucinatory under acute stress is medically immaterial; the *encoding* is the injury. Likely sequelae installed at this age: sleep-onset disturbance, enuresis (undocumented but probable in any Zefiro child of that period after such an event), startle-response hyperreactivity persisting into adulthood.

**Paternal loss (~age 7–8).** *Fantastic Four Annual* #2 establishes the canonical scene: Werner flees the Baron across a winter mountain with the boy bundled inside his own coat, dies of hypothermia having stripped his outer garments around the child. Subject wakes against a cold father. Direct somatic encoding: the **smell, weight, and temperature of a dead parent's body experienced as the only thing keeping him alive**. This is the somatic anchor of every subsequent "protector" pattern. Predictable adult sequelae, all observed: thermal intolerance toward cold (the armor is heated; Latverian throne rooms run warm), aversion to being held, aversion to embrace from above or behind. Probable mild frostbite to extremities at the time — undocumented, but the adult subject favors thick gauntlets even when finer manipulation is available, a soft tell of cold-memory in the hands.

---

## 2. ADOLESCENCE IN LATVERIA (~Year 8 — Year 16)

**Self-directed survival medicine.** Orphaned, the child raised himself among Zefiro remnants and in mountain caves, scavenging both Romani folk pharmacopoeia (likely yarrow, willow bark, comfrey poultice, mushroom-based febrifuges) and stolen Latverian field-medical supplies. He treated his own wounds from age eight or nine onward. Multiple scars on the hands, forearms, and shins inferred from this period — none documented because the patient never permits examination, but the *competence* of his later self-surgery (see §4) indicates a long apprenticeship in cutting and stitching his own flesh without anesthesia.

**Combat injuries, undocumented.** Guerrilla harassment of Fortunov's troops from approximately age twelve. Inferred injury inventory: at least one healed long-bone fracture (probably left ulna, parry fracture), multiple lacerations from edged weapons, at least one ballistic graze, repeated contusions. No professional setting of any of these injuries — they healed as they healed, which is to say imperfectly. The adult patient has a slightly stiffened left wrist that he conceals through gauntlet articulation.

**Pubertal development.** Normal, but compressed into an environment with no peer cohort and no female presence after Cynthia. The Valeria of Latveria attachment forms in this window — the *only* recorded peer relationship of the subject's life that predates the armor. Sexual development is consequently locked to a single idealized object, never broadened, and after her loss (functionally during the exile, definitively in *Unthinkable*) never re-opened. Subject is, by any reasonable inference, behaviorally celibate from approximately age twenty-two onward, with brief operational exceptions (Morgan le Fay; courtship of Sue Richards) that read as power-bids, not intimacies.

**Initial sorcerous exposure.** Possession and use of his mother's grimoires from early adolescence. Magical work at this developmental stage is, by every in-universe authority (Strange, Clea, the Aged Genghis), neurologically and somatically taxing — the patient is laying down mystical scar tissue before his prefrontal cortex has finished myelinating. This is one of two reasons his magic is forever "second to his science": the foundation was poured wrong.

---

## 3. EMPIRE STATE UNIVERSITY (~Year 16 — Year 18)

**Baseline medical intake (State Department, US entry).** Reconstructed: subject would have presented at intake as underweight for height, scarred, with elevated resting heart rate, untreated dentition, and a thoroughly abnormal psychiatric screen masked by exceptional cognitive performance. The screen was waived; he was a strategic asset.

**Sleep architecture.** Roommate-era reports (Reed, secondarily Ben) consistent across retellings: subject slept three to four hours, terminal insomnia, light-on, often at the workbench. This is not a study habit. This is post-traumatic hyperarousal with the lights kept on against the cold father on the mountain. The pattern persists for six decades.

**The Accident.** Dimensional-contact apparatus detonates in the subject's face. Objective injury per the unretconned record (Kirby pencils; Byrne reveal in *FF* #236; *Books of Doom* #2): **a single thin scar, roughly vertical, paramedian, perhaps four to seven centimeters, with associated periorbital singeing and possible first-degree flash burn**. No globe injury. No skeletal involvement. No airway compromise. Hospitalization brief. *This is the injury.* The catastrophic disfigurement universally attributed to "the accident" was not produced by it.

**Psychological encoding of the Accident.** The scar's medical triviality is inversely proportional to its psychological magnitude. The shame is generated not by the wound but by the *witnessing* — Reed having flagged the error, the Dean having expelled him, the laboratory peers having seen him fail in the one domain where failure was forbidden. The wound becomes a stigma in the religious sense: a visible mark of an invisible disgrace. The body cannot supply a wound proportional to the shame, so the body will be made to.

---

## 4. THE TIBETAN INTERVAL AND THE MASKING (~Year 19 — Year 21)

**Monastic conditioning.** Two to three years of disciplined ascesis under an unnamed Tibetan order. Documented effects: substantial gain in lean mass, mastery of breathwork sufficient to lower heart rate at will, pain-tolerance training, the beginnings of formal mystical practice integrated with the folk-magic foundation. Subject emerges physically transformed — broader, calmer in baseline, capable of the controlled stillness that becomes his diplomatic register.

**The armor fabrication.** Forged by his own hand from monastic-supplied materials. The metallurgy is exceptional; the workmanship suggests several hundred hours of focused craft. Each plate fits him specifically; the suit is anatomically bespoke and would fit no other body cleanly.

**The masking event.** *Astonishing Tales* #8 and the canonical visualization across writers: subject orders the monk to bring the mask before it has cooled and places it upon his own face. **The metal is cherry-hot — well above the point of full-thickness burn at any contact duration measurable in seconds.** The injuries thereby self-inflicted: full-thickness facial burns over the majority of the anterior face, partial preservation of the eyes (the mask's eye-cutouts spared the globes; the periorbital tissue did not survive intact), destruction of facial sebaceous and sweat architecture, near-total loss of facial hair follicles, scar contracture distorting the perioral and periocular musculature permanently.

**Operative read.** This is a self-mutilation event. It is performed by a man with two to three years of monastic affect-regulation training — i.e., it is *not* impulsive. It is the most premeditated act in the case file. The wound is engineered to match the shame: the subject required a face that *deserved* hiding, and constructed one. Pincus et al. (2009) frame grandiose narcissism as defense over a shame-driven interior; here the patient instantiates the defense *in tissue*. The mask is welded to the face metaphorically and almost so literally — the burn-scar topography from that moment forward becomes the substrate to which every future mask seats.

**Post-mask physiology.** Permanent loss of facial sweating means thermoregulation must be managed by armor systems; this is one of several functional reasons the armor cannot come off. Permanent loss of full facial expression means social signaling routes entirely through voice, posture, and gauntlet gesture — and the patient is exceptionally good at all three, having had no other channel for forty-plus years. Likely chronic pain: trigeminal involvement from scar contracture, low-grade ocular surface disease from impaired blinking, chronic temporomandibular dysfunction from the rigid mask seating against the mandible.

---

## 5. THE ARMORED DECADES — CHRONIC SOMATIC PATTERN

**Continuous encasement.** From approximately age twenty-one to the present, the subject is in armor more than 95% of waking hours. Documented effects:

- *Musculoskeletal.* Servo-augmented load distribution means his native musculature is *less* developed than his apparent strength suggests. Out of armor he is strong — six feet two, broad, conditioned by lifelong asceticism — but not at the level his armored performance implies. Long-term postural lock from the suit's collar geometry: cervical range of motion is reduced; he turns from the shoulders.
- *Dermatological.* Chronic occlusion dermatitis under armor liners, managed by a rotating set of medicated underweaves of his own design. Likely chronic intertriginous candidiasis in flexural zones absent active management. The subject is fastidious about this; aides reconstruct elaborate decontamination rituals between armor sessions.
- *Proprioceptive.* Six decades of armored proprioception has rewritten his body schema. Out of armor he is documentably *clumsy* — his hands reach where the gauntlets would terminate, not where his fingers terminate. He has not, in adulthood, possessed an unmediated sense of his own physical extent.
- *Sensory.* He has not felt unfiltered wind on his face, direct sunlight on his skin, or another person's hand on his cheek since approximately age twenty-one. *By choice.* This is sensory deprivation as identity maintenance. The clinical consequence is a profound deafening of the affiliative-touch system; affection arrives only through visual or auditory channels and is correspondingly easy to misread as performance.
- *Vestibular.* The helmet damps ambient sound and creates a constant low-frequency resonance against the skull. Subject's auditory environment is acoustically *his own*. Removal of the helmet, on the rare occasions it occurs, produces a brief disorientation he conceals.

**Diet.** Per Hickman and Waid characterization: ascetic, ritualized, low-volume, scheduled. Probable composition — high-protein, low-glycemic, micronutrient-supplemented, no alcohol, no caffeine, no stimulants. He eats alone. He eats unmasked, briefly, in chambers swept for surveillance. The act of eating is the most regular vulnerability in his daily cycle and is correspondingly the most protected.

**Sleep.** Three to five hours nightly, fragmented, light-cued. Frequent parasomnias inferable from staff accounts of nocturnal workshop activity. Recurrent dream content (his mother burning, his father cold) is not documented in his voice but is overdetermined.

**Cardiovascular.** Resting heart rate trained low by monastic discipline; reactivity to specific stimuli (the Richards name; mention of the mother; the mask referenced) is sharp. The differential — calm before Galactus, tachycardic at a smirk — is the autonomic signature of trauma-cued dysregulation along a narrow axis, consistent with van Dijke et al. (2018) on C-PTSD identity-alteration as stimulus-bounded rather than diffuse.

---

## 6. TRANSFORMATIONS, BODY-SWAPS, DISMEMBERMENTS, RESURRECTIONS

**Body-swap with Reed Richards (*FF* #10).** Subject inhabits Richards's body. Reports — i.e., the absence of subsequent reports — are diagnostic. The patient never speaks of this event again. The experience of being *inside* the rival's body, of moving as Reed moves, of being addressed as Reed by Reed's wife and friends, of *not being recognized as himself by anyone who claimed to love Reed* — this is a narcissistic injury of unusual specificity (he wanted to be Reed and discovered no one noticed Reed was gone, which is to say no one would notice if *he* were gone, which is to say the central premise of his existence — that he is unmissably significant — is falsifiable). It is sealed and never reopened. This is not absence of impact; it is the depth of impact requiring total occlusion.

**Power Cosmic acquisitions (*FF* #57–60, and subsequently).** Temporary uploads of cosmic-tier energy through his nervous system. Each event leaves residual mystical-energetic scarring detectable, per Strange's commentary in *Triumph and Torment*, on the subject's astral signature. Cumulative effect: the subject's soul, considered as a measurable object in his universe, is *scarred tissue* — not pristine, not damned outright, but worn thin in patches.

**Beyonder-power assumption, *Secret Wars* (1984), and divestiture.** Apotheosis followed by self-engineered loss because the unconscious self-image could not host the conscious self-claim. Somatic correlate: documented post-event collapse, weeks of recovery. The patient's own physiology rejected the godhood his armor demanded he claim.

**Soul transactions with Mephisto.** Annual ritual (*Astonishing Tales* #8 onward) of attempted maternal rescue. Each failure produces attritional damage — Strange's later assessment is that the cumulative mystical injury would have crippled a lesser practitioner. The patient absorbs the damage as further proof that he must continue, the loss of capacity becoming itself a reason to escalate.

**Disembodiment and reconstitution events.** Multiple, across decades — armor-only persistence after corporeal destruction; reconstitution via prepared contingencies; the Hickman-era reintegrations. Each event teaches the body that it is *replaceable*, which deepens the identification with the mask (which is *not* replaceable, because the mask is the self).

**The Maker / Infamous Iron Man interval (Bendis 2016–2018).** Facial cosmesis restored — the subject possesses, briefly, a face. *He cannot tolerate it.* Behavioral evidence: increasing dysregulation across the arc, eventual return to scarred presentation and to armor. The unscarred face is dysphoric to him in the strict clinical sense — it does not match the somatic identity, which is locked to disfigurement. This is the strongest single piece of evidence that the burn-injury is *constitutive* of the self, not incidental to it. A face without the wound is not his face.

**Triumph and Torment (1989).** Mother freed; subject undergoes a brief integration — observable in the artwork as a slight postural softening, a register-shift in speech — and then is repudiated by the freed mother. The somatic response is rage at Mephisto and physical assault on the demon; the psychic response is reconsolidation of the armor within weeks. The window closes. The patient experienced a moment of post-traumatic relief and could not metabolize it.

**Secret Wars (2015) god-state.** Multi-year occupancy of omnipotent god-emperor function. Physiological correlate inferable: the body, supported by Beyonder-tier energetics, did not age, did not require maintenance, did not feel pain. *He gave it up.* The concession to Reed at the close — "you would have done it better" — is the single most clinically significant utterance in the file, and lasts approximately one issue before the defense system overwrites it.

---

## 7. SURGICAL HISTORY (KNOWN AND INFERRED)

No record of submission to external surgery in adulthood. All procedures upon the subject's body since approximately age twenty-one have been performed either by the subject himself or by Doombot-mediated automation under the subject's direct control. Inferred procedure log:

- Self-administered cybernetic integration of armor neural interfaces (multiple revisions across decades).
- Self-administered debridement and management of recurrent armor-occlusion dermatoses.
- Self-administered minor orthopedic and dental work.
- Probable self-administered ocular surface management for chronic exposure keratopathy secondary to the masking burns.
- Self-administered or Doombot-administered repair of combat injuries, including at least one full thoracic-cavity reconstruction inferable from the survival of injuries that would have killed an unequipped subject.

The refusal to be operated on by another hand is itself a symptom: it is the same refusal that produced the masking event. *No one's hands but his own may shape his body.*

---

## 8. SUBSTANCES

No documented use of alcohol, recreational drugs, tobacco, or caffeine. No documented use of pharmaceutical psychotropics. No documented use of performance-enhancing compounds beyond his own engineered metabolic supports. This abstention is *total* and is not framed as health behavior — it is framed, when framed at all, as a refusal to permit any agent to occupy a position of influence over his cognition that he has not personally vetted and built. *The patient is phobic of impaired control.* The abstinence is a defense, not a virtue.

Secondary inference: the subject's relationship to ingestion of *anything* (food, drink, air) is tightly managed. He does not accept refreshment at others' tables when politically possible to refuse. The hospitality of foreign powers is consumed by body-doubles or analyzed and replicated by his own kitchens. The childhood loss of the mother to poison-by-power-bargain and the father to a poisoning of trust by the Baron leave a long shadow on what enters the body.

---

## 9. NEUROLOGICAL AND COGNITIVE STATUS

No record of stroke, seizure disorder, or neurodegenerative process. Cognitive performance across six decades is preserved at exceptional baseline — eidetic recall consistent, working-memory capacity vast, executive function intact under most loads. Cognitive flexibility is documentably *reduced* under ego-threat (will pursue a known-losing line rather than reverse), which is a personality-level phenomenon rather than a neurological deficit, but it has neurological *expression* — prefrontal regulation yields to limbic drive at shame-triggers in a stereotyped, reproducible pattern. This is the C-PTSD signature operating beneath the NPD surface.

Mystical practice has produced what Strange has characterized as a kind of dual-processing cognitive style — the subject thinks scientifically and magically in parallel, integrating both streams into single decisions. This integration is *rare* in his universe and is one of his genuine cognitive distinctions.

---

## 10. SOMATIC IDENTITY — INTEGRATIVE NOTE

The medical history of this subject cannot be read as a sequence of injuries to a body. It must be read as the *construction of a body to match a self-concept*. The accident provided a scratch; the patient supplied the disfigurement. The armor provides the protection; the patient supplied the imprisonment. The magic provides power; the patient supplied the attritional damage. The kingdom provides the throne; the patient supplied the solitude in which he eats.

Every somatic fact in this file is, at root, the same fact: the body has been organized — surgically, behaviorally, ritually, architecturally — to be a fortress around a child on a mountain against a cold father, and a fortress around a boy in a laboratory whose calculation may have been wrong. The body is doing what the mind cannot afford to do, which is *remember directly*. Restore the face and the structure trembles. Remove the armor and the proprioception fails. Free the mother and the system reconsolidates within weeks because the structure has no other purpose. The somatic identity is locked to the wound because the wound is the only honest thing about him, and he knows it, which is why it must never be examined.

— End medical history. Cross-refer §3 (Psychological), §4 (Psychiatric) of analytical workup for affective and structural correlates of each somatic finding above.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: VICTOR VON DOOM

*File segment 04-B. Granular bodily record. All observations cross-referenced against direct surveillance, satellite thermography, audio capture from Latverian state functions, and the testimony of the small handful of persons who have seen the subject unmasked and survived to be debriefed. Read in conjunction with Medical (§2) and Psychological (§3).*

---

## I. THE ARMOR AS BODY

The first methodological note for any analyst opening this file: the subject does not have a body in the ordinary sense. He has a **body-armor composite**, continuous for so long that the boundary is no longer meaningful. The flesh has shaped to the steel and the steel has been re-machined to the flesh — micro-tolerances re-measured, by Doom's own hand in his workshop, on a quarterly cycle that coincides with the lunar feast days observed by the Zefiro of his childhood (this calendar alignment is unspoken and almost certainly unconscious; he has never named it).

The armor weighs an estimated 180–220 kg in standard configuration. Without servo-augmentation he could not stand in it for more than a few minutes; this is not a weakness he experiences as one, because he is never without the servos. **He has not voluntarily stood in unaugmented gravity, on bare feet, on natural ground, for at least thirty years.** When he does — in *Triumph and Torment*'s pilgrimage to Strange's sanctum, in the brief Hickman-era walks through the Latverian foothills — he wobbles for the first three steps and then over-corrects into a stiffness that reads to subordinates as imperious and to a trained eye as proprioceptive recalibration. He is, in effect, a deep-sea creature surfacing.

Therefore: **most of what follows is the armor's behavior, because the armor is the body.** A separate sub-section addresses what is known of the flesh underneath.

---

## II. STANCE AND POSTURE

**Standing baseline.** Feet shoulder-width, weight evenly distributed across both heels with a barely perceptible forward bias of ~3°. Spine drawn vertical to the point of slight retroflexion at the lumbar — a posture that reads as imperial because it *is* an imperial posture; he learned it deliberately, in the Tibetan monastery, from murals of god-kings, and has held it for fifty years. The shoulders are squared but not braced; the brace is in the lats, not the trapezius, which means the readable line is calm rather than tense.

**Hands at rest.** Almost always clasped at the small of the back when not actively engaged — a parade-rest variant. When seated on the throne, hands grip the chair's terminal lions at the second knuckle, never the first; never the palm. When standing without the cloak about him, the right hand rests in a loose claw three centimeters from the holstered blaster on the right thigh-plate; the left hangs straight. **He never lets both hands hang at his sides simultaneously for more than four seconds**; one is always doing something, even if only suspended in a gesture of contemplation at his chin-plate.

**Cloak management.** A continuous low-grade motor pattern. The cloak is heavy (lined with chainmesh) and he manipulates it constantly: a sweeping clearance of the right arm before any technical work; a left-hand draw across the body when seated, the cloth pulled tight to the opposite knee in an unconscious self-swaddling that intensifies under emotional pressure. **Surveillance correlation: cloak-drawn-across-body in seated position is the most reliable single tell of incipient distress.** In moments of triumph he lets it fall fully open and behind him; in moments of shame he gathers it across his torso like a child's blanket and is unaware he has done so.

**Sitting.** Throne: spine off the back-rest by a fixed two centimeters at all times. He never relaxes against the seat. Even in private — confirmed by his own diaries, which he writes seated at a desk — he keeps the lumbar lifted. Sleeping seated has been observed; sleeping reclined has not been confirmed in the surveillance window.

**Kneeling.** Performed only twice in the recorded canon and both times under duress (before Mephisto; before the In-Betweener). Both instances were followed within forty-eight hours by displays of extravagant cruelty that read as **counter-shame discharge**.

---

## III. GAIT

**Standard.** A measured 1.1 m/s, almost metronomic, the stride length unvarying to within five centimeters across thousands of recorded paces. The armored boots strike heel-first with deliberate sonic weight — he has *tuned* the resonance of the floor in the throne hall to amplify the step. He walks across his own architecture as a performance. The footfall pattern does not change when he believes himself unobserved; the performance is for himself as well.

**Accelerated.** When moving with purpose toward a workshop or laboratory, the stride lengthens by approximately fifteen percent and the cloak begins to flow behind him in a manner he has practiced before mirrors (mirror-practice confirmed by the Hauptmann debriefs and by the polished obsidian panels in his private gallery, which are angled for self-observation under the pretense of being decorative).

**Combat.** Economical, low-amplitude footwork, **never bounces** — the center of gravity stays at a constant height above the floor. He is one of the few combatants in the recorded files who does not telegraph weight transfer because his armor's gyroscopes will not let him. He fights from the hips and from the wrists; the shoulders barely move.

**Limping or favoring.** When injured, the limp is suppressed by armor compensation in public and indulged in private — a fact established by stride-asymmetry analysis of corridor sensor data after the events of *Triumph and Torment*. The public gait was perfect; the private gait, walking alone in the gallery at 03:14 local, dragged the left leg by 11 cm/stride.

---

## IV. HANDS

**Doom's hands are the most expressive part of the somatic record** because the face is locked. The mask telegraphs nothing; the hands telegraph everything that escapes.

- **The cathedral.** Fingertips pressed together at chest height while listening. Held when the speaker is being weighed. Disengaged abruptly the moment a judgment is reached.
- **The sweep.** A flat right-hand sweep, palm down, that closes a topic. Used to dismiss subordinates, to silence the Cabal, to end audiences. The sweep is from the centerline outward to the right; he has never been observed to do it leftward.
- **The slow close.** The gauntlet curls into a fist over a ten-to-fifteen-second interval when Reed Richards is named in his presence. The curl is *not* into a striking fist; the thumb stays atop the index, not over it. It is a containing fist. He is holding something in, not preparing to throw something out.
- **The two-finger tap.** Right index and middle finger tapped against the left forearm-plate at irregular intervals when bored. This is the only random-rhythm motion in his entire somatic repertoire and accordingly the most informative — boredom is a state he tolerates poorly and the tap is the visible edge of an internal monologue racing.
- **Workshop hands.** Inside the workshop he removes the outer gauntlets and works in inner gloves — fine, articulated, almost surgical. The gestures here are *small*, precise, with a luthier's economy. Watching him solder is watching a different man. **This is the only context in which his hands move below the level of his hips.**
- **Gauntleted touch of another person.** Extraordinarily rare. When he touches Valeria Richards (the child) on the head or shoulder — recorded thrice in the Waid run — the gauntlet is *removed* first. The act of removing the gauntlet for a child is, in the entire surveillance record, unique to her. He has never removed the gauntlet to shake another adult's hand.

**The flesh of the hands.** Beneath the gloves: scarred from the same forge that produced the armor; calloused at the pads in patterns that map to soldering iron, screwdriver, brush (he paints, badly), saber hilt. The nails are kept short and square. There is a thin ring of paler skin on the left fourth finger that no canonical wedding accounts for — a vestige of the unsuccessful Sue Storm timeline of *Secret Wars* (2015), somatically remembered.

---

## V. THE FACE AND THE MASK

**The mask is the face.** The metal is articulated at the jaw to permit speech but does not move with expression; there is no expression to move with. **The eyeholes are the only readable feature**, and they read by *darkness behavior*: the depth of shadow visible inside is modulated by his head-tilt, which he uses, consciously or otherwise, like a cuttlefish uses chromatophores. Head lowered three degrees: shadow deepens, threat reading. Head raised three degrees: light enters the eyeholes, the audience can see he is looking at them, audience reading.

**Head tilts (catalogued).**
- *The cock to the right, 8°:* I am considering whether you have just insulted me.
- *The slow lower, 4°:* You have, and you will not survive the next sentence unless it corrects.
- *The lift, 6°, with cloak-clearance of right arm:* I am about to speak at length; do not interrupt.
- *The full forward lean from the throne, hands on knee-plates:* This concerns my mother. Choose your next word.

**Beneath the mask.** Sources who have seen the face report what the medical file confirms: the *actual* scarring is modest. A thin diagonal at the left temple, faint puckering along the jaw — the kind of mark a vain man hides with a beard. The catastrophic burn-pattern across the rest of the face was self-administered when he set the white-hot mask onto unprepared skin. The healed result, decades on, is a face of which he can speak only in the third person. He **does not look at his own face**. The mirrors in his private quarters are angled to show the mask only; the polished panels in the gallery show the silhouette. The two confirmed unmasking events in the past decade were each followed by hours alone in a sealed room, after which the armor was re-donned and the room was destroyed by his own hand.

**The voice.** Resonant baritone, projected from the chest, with the mask's acoustics adding a metallic upper formant. He has trained the voice as carefully as the posture. Under stress the cadence does not break — it *lengthens*, syllables drawn fractionally longer, vowels held a beat past natural. This is the audio analogue of cloak-drawing: the slower he speaks, the more he is concealing. **Genuine calm sounds clipped; performed calm sounds slow.** The third-person construction ("Doom does not…") functions partly as a metrical device — it gives him an extra foot in every sentence to compose the next.

**Laughter.** Three documented kinds. (i) *The proclamation laugh,* HA-HA-HA, three beats, performative, used in victory tableaux and reliably hollow. (ii) *The single huff* through the mask's vocoder, brief, dry, used at genuine irony — most often in conversation with Strange. (iii) *The unguarded laugh,* recorded twice, both with Valeria Richards present, both quickly suppressed; brief, low, and unexpectedly warm, originating from the diaphragm rather than the throat.

---

## VI. GROOMING AND DAILY MAINTENANCE

The grooming schedule of a man whose face is hidden is not what an outsider would assume. It is more, not less, fastidious.

**Daily.** Pre-dawn, before any servant is admitted. The mask is removed, the face cleaned with a specific lanolin-based ointment (Latverian formulary, of his own design, containing topical analgesic for the chronic neuralgia in the burn margins), the chamois beneath the chin-plate replaced. The hair — present, dark, lightly silvered at the temples, kept at a short military length by his own clipper — is washed in a basin, never under running water (a Zefiro habit, preserved across all transformations). Teeth: cleaned with a Latverian dentifrice of mint and clove, twice daily, with obsessive thoroughness. He has perfect teeth; nobody sees them.

**Weekly.** Armor disassembled in part and re-tolerance-checked. Skin examined for pressure sores at the seven contact points (occiput, upper trapezius bilateral, sacrum, ischial tuberosities bilateral, dorsum of foot bilateral). Existing sores are dressed with the same lanolin ointment.

**Cyclical.** Quarterly full re-machining of the armor against his measured body — referenced above against the Zefiro lunar calendar. Annual replacement of the mask itself, the old mask retained in a sealed reliquary in the lower gallery. There are now forty-plus masks in that reliquary, dated, in order. He visits the reliquary at most once a year, on the anniversary of his mother's death.

**The cloak.** Hand-washed by Doom himself, never by a servant, in a stone basin in the workshop. The act of washing the cloak is one of the few recorded instances of him performing menial labor. It takes approximately ninety minutes. He does it without music, without speech, in absolute concentration. This is, by every behavioral metric available, **a meditation ritual that he would deny if named.**

---

## VII. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Total nightly sleep:** estimated four to five hours, fragmented into two blocks.

**Block one: 22:00–01:30.** Seated, in a high-backed chair in his private study, armor partially relaxed (gauntlets off, helm hinged back but not removed). He calls this "rest, not sleep." EEG correlate (inferred from medical scans during the Reckoning War recovery period) suggests stage 2 NREM achieved, REM rare in this block.

**Block two: 04:00–06:00.** Recumbent, in a low cot in an adjoining chamber, armor fully removed, body covered in a heavy wool blanket of Zefiro weave (the only surviving textile from his childhood enclave; this fact is unrecorded in any non-classified source). Block two contains the REM. **Nightmares are reliably present**, evidenced by audio capture: muttered Romani, the words *mama, papa, the cold,* once *Reed, please*. He does not remember the dreams on waking, or claims not to.

**Wake protocol.** 06:00 sharp, no alarm, internal. The first conscious act is a thirty-second ritual at the cot's edge — head bowed, hands on knees, breathing slowed to four cycles per minute. He has performed this at every recorded wake-instance. He has never explained it. The probability that it is a prayer of some kind, addressed to his mother, approaches certainty.

**Sleep degradation under stress.** During active Richards confrontations, block two collapses entirely; block one extends with stimulant tea (a Latverian preparation of his own composition, not caffeine — derived from a mountain herb) and the recumbent period is replaced by pacing. Across a typical Reed-cycle (4–9 days from initial incident to resolution), he loses 6–8 kg of body mass and the post-event recovery requires roughly twice the duration of the event itself.

---

## VIII. EATING

**Mode.** Almost always alone. State banquets are attended for political function; he sits at the head of the table and does not eat in front of guests — the mask remains in place, a goblet is touched to its lower rim, food is moved on the plate. He eats afterward, in a small chamber off the kitchens.

**Diet.** Spartan. Black bread (a Zefiro recipe, baked daily by a hereditary palace baker whose family has been in the role for four generations and who is paid more than any general). Hard cheese. A clear vegetable broth at midday. Roast meat once weekly, on the Latverian sabbath. Honeyed walnuts as a private indulgence — kept in a small lacquer box in the workshop. Wine refused.

**Eating posture.** Seated upright, no music, no reading material. The meal is finished in under twelve minutes. Utensils handled with the same economy as the workshop instruments.

**Stress shifts.** Under prolonged stress the diet narrows further; he will subsist for days on broth and bread alone. After a major victory, the honeyed walnuts appear on the workshop bench. Subordinates have learned to read the empty lacquer box as a barometer of psychological state — full box: stable to negative; emptied box: he has scored against a major rival.

---

## IX. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

**Sexual record:** sparse and tightly controlled. Confirmed intimate liaisons include Valeria of Latveria (pre-armor, terminated by his own withdrawal); Morgan le Fay (instrumental, magical-political); and the constructed-domestic arrangement with Sue Storm under the *Secret Wars* (2015) interregnum (which was kept *chaste in his own architecture* — a datum that is itself diagnostic: given infinite power, he reconstructed marriage but not the marriage bed).

**Physical intimacy reading.** Subject is **touch-averse to the point of phobia** with adults, **touch-tolerant** with the child Valeria Richards, **touch-instrumental** with subordinates (a hand on the shoulder as benediction, withdrawn within two seconds). The aversion is not desire-absence — it is exposure-aversion. To be touched is to be located, measured, known. The armor is, among everything else, a chastity device of a specifically narcissistic kind: it makes the body unavailable for evaluation.

**Arousal indicators (such as can be inferred):** rare, displaced, and almost always cued by *power-coded* stimuli rather than person-coded ones. The body responds to throne, to oath-taking, to the moment of a defeated rival's acknowledgment; it does not, by the available record, respond to undress or proximity. Romantic gestures, when performed, are *iconographic*: roses sent, sonnets written (yes, recorded — they exist in a locked drawer; they are competent and cold), tokens delivered.

**Withdrawal pattern after intimacy.** Documented in the Valeria-of-Latveria thread and the brief Sue-Storm domestic period: a measurable retreat into work within hours, followed by a compensatory display of dominance toward a third party within days. Closeness must be paid for, immediately, by an act that reaffirms supremacy.

---

## X. MICRO-MOVEMENT REPERTOIRE BY STATE

**State 1 — Calm (governance, lecture, technical work).**
- Breath: 8–10 cpm, diaphragmatic, audible through mask vocoder as a low and even baseline.
- Head: minimal tilt, eyes track speaker.
- Hands: cathedral or behind back.
- Cloak: open, undisturbed.
- Voice: clipped, didactic, third-person but conversational in pace.
- Tell: the two-finger tap if duration exceeds his interest.

**State 2 — Mild challenge.**
- Breath unchanged; *control of breath* is the dominant defense.
- Head: 3–8° cock to the right.
- Hands: slow close of the right gauntlet.
- Cloak: left hand begins gathering at the hip.
- Voice: slows by ~15%, vowels lengthen.
- Tell: a single, deliberate exhalation through the vocoder before reply.

**State 3 — Competence questioned.**
- Breath: deepens by 20%, still controlled.
- Head: lowered 4°, eyeholes darken.
- Hands: full containing fist, right. The left rises to the chin-plate.
- Cloak: gathered fully across torso if seated; flared if standing (the binary choice is involuntary and reads accurately as defensive vs. aggressive posture).
- Voice: drops by a third in pitch, gains the upper metallic formant.
- Tell: he stops using contractions entirely. "I will" not "I'll." "Doom does not" not "Doom doesn't."

**State 4 — Shame surfacing.**
- Breath: irregular for the first time, a single held inhalation followed by accelerated cycle.
- Head: motion increases — small lateral oscillations, ~2° each, at 1–2 Hz, the only recurring tremor in the somatic record. **This head-shimmer is the single most reliable indicator of imminent self-sabotage.**
- Hands: the slow close becomes a striking fist; gauntlet seams flex audibly.
- Cloak: torn through, abandoned, or flung — a sudden costume change at the moment shame breaks containment.
- Voice: rises a half-step, breaks into monologue, demands acknowledgment. The third-person construction *intensifies* — "DOOM" is invoked four to six times per minute, up from baseline 0.5.
- Tell: he begins to *gesture toward* the opponent rather than at them, an opened palm thrust forward, fingers spread — a posture of presentation, as if showing the universe a wound.

**State 5 — Exposure of the wounded self (rare; *Triumph and Torment* finale, *Secret Wars* 2015 finale, *Unthinkable* climax).**
- Breath: dysregulated, gasping audible through vocoder.
- Head: bowed fully forward, mask angled toward floor — the eyeholes show no light at all.
- Hands: drop. **Both hands at his sides simultaneously**, which has been noted as the four-second prohibition; sustained drop indicates collapse.
- Cloak: ignored. May trail in mud, in blood.
- Voice: drops to first-person. **The shift from third- to first-person pronoun is the deepest somatic-linguistic event in the entire file.** He has said "I" perhaps a dozen times in sixty years. Each instance is logged. Each preceded a significant rupture or a brief integration.
- Tell: a single slow exhale, prolonged past the breath's natural end, the lungs emptied. Followed almost invariably by violence directed outward, *not* at the witness of the shame but at a substitute target — wall, furniture, lesser opponent — and by destruction of any recording device in the vicinity.

**State 6 — Intimacy (rare; child-coded).**
- Breath: deepens and slows beyond baseline.
- Head: lowered to the child's eye-level — a posture he assumes for no other purpose.
- Hands: ungauntleted, motion small and slow, the workshop register applied to a small body. He has been observed adjusting Valeria Richards's collar with the same care he uses to seat a circuit.
- Cloak: drawn around the child once, briefly, in cold weather, recorded by external camera at the periphery of a Latverian visit. He was unaware of the camera.
- Voice: drops in volume by a full register, loses the vocoder's upper formant entirely (he angles the mask so the sound reaches her chest-level rather than through the projecting grille). Speaks in nearly full sentences without third-person construction. **In Valeria's presence, "I" returns naturally.** This is the only social context in which it does.
- Tell: he lingers. The four-second hand-drop prohibition lapses. The cathedral position dissolves. For brief intervals — never longer than two minutes — the armor contains a man rather than a monument.

---

## XI. THE WOUNDED CHILD'S BODY, RESIDUAL

A short concluding note for the analyst. Beneath every layer above — the imperial posture, the metronomic gait, the controlled breath, the rationed laugh — there is a body that learned its first lessons running through a Latverian winter, hiding in stone barns, watching its father die of cold against its own small back. **The thermoregulation patterns persist.** He keeps his thro


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

*Dossier Section 7 of 14. Cross-reference §1 (History), §3 (Psychological), §4 (Psychiatric). Behavioral substantiation drawn from canonical record 1962–present.*

---

## 7.1 Attachment Classification and Its Origins

The subject presents a **disorganized attachment** with a heavy **dismissive-avoidant overlay** and intermittent **fearful-avoidant** breakthroughs under shame load. The classification is not a guess; it is the only configuration that survives the longitudinal evidence.

The originating template is unambiguous. Cynthia von Doom — competent, loving, lethal in her competence — disappears into Hell *because* of her love for her son and her people. Werner von Doom — competent, loving, helpless against power — dies on a winter mountain *shielding his son with his own body* after his competence (medical skill) fails to save a tyrant's wife. The child Victor, between ages roughly six and ten, sustains a sequence of inputs that no developing attachment system can metabolize:

- **The loved caregiver is annihilated** (not merely lost — *damned*, in the mother's case; *dead of exposure on the child's behalf*, in the father's).
- **The annihilation is caused by the love itself.** Cynthia bargains for power *to protect Victor and the Zefiro*; that bargain damns her. Werner refuses to flee without Victor; that refusal kills him.
- **The protector dies in physical contact with the child.** Werner's body, cold against Victor's, is the last sustained skin-to-skin contact the subject is known to permit in his entire life. The next deliberate touch to his face will be the white-hot mask.
- **There is no successor caregiver.** The Zefiro provide tribal cover but not parental function. Boris, the loyal retainer, enters later and is permitted only the role of servant-uncle, never parent.

From this the internal working model crystallizes: **closeness is the murder-weapon used against the loved object; the only safe attachment is to the dead-idealized parent and to one's own omnipotent future self.** Bowlby's "internal working model" here becomes a closed theorem rather than a living hypothesis — the child's grief is solved by the construction of a self that *cannot be lost because it cannot be reached.*

This is the soil from which the mask grows. The mask is not metaphor for the attachment system; it *is* the attachment system, externalized in titanium.

---

## 7.2 How the Subject Bonds

Bonding, when it occurs, follows a strict and observable protocol.

**Initial filtering.** The subject sorts every new dyad into one of five bins within seconds: *rival*, *subordinate*, *peer-equal* (rare), *child-coded ward*, or *instrumental cipher*. The sort is irreversible without cataclysmic data; once binned, a person is treated according to the script for that bin for decades. Reed Richards was binned *rival* at age eighteen and has never been re-binned despite multiple alliances, shared sons-in-law in spirit (Valeria Richards), and joint world-savings.

**Bonding by oath, not by disclosure.** The subject does not bond by mutual vulnerability — the standard adult intimacy protocol. He bonds by **sworn obligation**. Boris is bound by feudal oath sworn back to Cynthia's era; Kristoff Vernard is adopted by formal decree; Doctor Strange is held in wary regard because of an oath honored at the door of Hell (*Triumph and Torment*, 1989); even his hostility to Richards is structured as a kind of inverted oath — a vow of permanent enmity, treated as binding. **The subject's relational glue is contractual, not affective.** This is consistent with C-PTSD identity organization (van Dijke et al. 2018): the patient bonds at the level of identity-role rather than at the level of feeling-state, because feeling-states are coded as the channel through which annihilation entered.

**Asymmetry as precondition.** Genuine bond formation requires a stable vertical relation — the subject above or, in the rarest case, openly below (only Cynthia in memory, briefly Strange in the underworld). Horizontal bonds — friendships of equals — do not form. The closest approximations are with Strange and T'Challa, and both are managed by elaborate ritual that *prevents* the relation from settling into the horizontal.

**The child exception.** Children bypass the protocol entirely. With Kristoff (pre-conditioning) and with Valeria Richards (Waid's run, *Fantastic Four* vol. 3 #67ff. and across the Hickman-era *Future Foundation*), an unguarded warmth leaks through — patient, gentle, instructive, and visibly *enjoyed* by the subject in a register he displays nowhere else. This is the buried Werner-template surfacing: he becomes, for a child, the protector his father was, with the addition of the power his father lacked. **A child in the room is the only consistent stimulus that produces unmasked affect.** It is also the only stimulus he afterward systematically denies, which is the second half of the diagnostic pattern.

---

## 7.3 How the Subject Distrusts

Distrust is the baseline state; trust is a localized exception. The architecture of distrust is layered:

**Layer 1 — Surveillance.** Doombots monitor Latveria continuously; the subject is briefed on essentially every meaningful interaction within his borders. This is not paranoia in the clinical sense; it is the *behavioral residue* of having once been a powerless child watching soldiers come for his mother. Knowledge precedes action; never again will information asymmetry be used against him.

**Layer 2 — Redundancy.** The subject keeps multiple Doombots of himself in circulation precisely so that no single betrayal can reach the real him. The Doombot architecture is, among other things, an **attachment prosthesis**: he can permit subordinates and even intimates to interact with "him" while the actual subject remains physically isolated. Visiting dignitaries have negotiated with Doombots for hours; loyal servants have served Doombots tea for days. The intimacy a normal monarch would extend is dispatched by proxy.

**Layer 3 — Recall and grievance ledger.** The subject maintains, internally, a meticulous account of every slight, every doubt, every smirk. Grievances older than fifty years are recalled with full affective freshness — the Empire State expulsion, Reed's calculation note, the dean's tone. This is not rumination in the depressive sense; it is **archival**, a defensive database against future minimization of the wound.

**Layer 4 — Provocation testing.** New entrants to his orbit are tested — given small lies to detect, minor authority to abuse, tempting confidences to leak. Failure is permanent demotion or removal; success rarely promotes, because *passing the test only earns the next test*. Boris has been passing tests for half a century without graduating from "trusted servant" to "intimate."

**The Richards exception to the distrust pattern.** The subject *trusts Reed Richards' competence absolutely* — will collaborate with him on cosmic threats without insisting on verification (Hickman's Council of Reeds; the Reckoning War). This is a tell. He distrusts Reed's *intentions toward Doom's self-image*, never Reed's *capacity*. The exception confirms the rule: distrust is shame-mediated, not threat-mediated. Where Reed cannot wound the self-image (e.g., shared work against Galactus), Reed is the most trusted person in the subject's life. Where Reed *can* wound it, no relation on Earth is more closely guarded.

---

## 7.4 How the Subject Betrays

The subject's betrayals follow a signature that distinguishes him from antisocial structures (cf. §4 differential).

**He does not betray oaths.** Sworn word is sacred; the brittleness of this code has been tested repeatedly across canon and held (e.g., his honoring of the Strange contract in *Triumph and Torment* even when honoring it humiliated him; his honoring of guest-right with the FF when they entered Latveria under safe-conduct, even where killing them would have been trivial). This is not morality in the warm sense; it is **the one zone where his pure will alone can produce order**, and he refuses to corrupt it.

**He betrays the unsworn.** Anyone outside the oath-network is fair game for instrumental sacrifice. The most disturbing canonical instance is the murder and *skin-wearing* of Valeria of Latveria, his childhood love, in *Unthinkable* (Waid, *FF* vol. 3 #67–70, 2003) — converted into demonic armor as price of magical power. Note the structure: he loved her; he had not *sworn* to her. The absence of oath converted her into available raw material under sufficient ego pressure.

**He betrays himself.** This is the most frequent and least obvious. At the apex of victories (the Beyonder power; the Battleworld dominion) he engineers his own collapse — see §1, Recurrent Self-Sabotage. The unconscious self-concept executes a betrayal of the conscious self-concept whenever the conscious self-concept threatens to be confirmed. *The subject betrays his own grandiosity to protect his shame core from disconfirmation*, because disconfirmation of the shame core would require him to grieve, and grief was the affect that, in childhood, accompanied annihilation.

**He betrays witnesses to his shame.** Doombots that observe him unmasked are destroyed; technicians who repair the suit are memory-wiped or rotated out of access; servants who walk in on the wrong moment vanish into reassignment. This is not cruelty for its own sake but **environmental hygiene** — the removal of the external record so that only his own (curated) internal record persists.

---

## 7.5 How the Subject Repairs

Repair, when it occurs, is **unilateral, indirect, and never named**.

The subject will not apologize. The word does not appear in his speech register across six decades of recorded dialogue except in extremis (the *Secret Wars* 2015 finale — "Reed… you would have been better" — a sentence the patient could only produce in the moment of literally losing the universe, and which he overwrote within weeks). Apology would constitute the explicit acknowledgment of fallibility his entire defensive structure exists to prevent.
